    WHERE "o"."Id" = @__orderId_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS "t"
LEFT JOIN "DistributeLoad" AS "d" ON "t"."OrderId0" = "d"."LoadingId"
LEFT JOIN "AxialForceLoad" AS "a" ON "t"."OrderId0" = "a"."LoadingId"
LEFT JOIN "EndMomentLoad" AS "e" ON "t"."OrderId0" = "e"."LoadingId"
LEFT JOIN "XPointLoad" AS "x" ON "t"."OrderId0" = "x"."LoadingId"
ORDER BY "t"."Id", "t"."OrderId", "t"."OrderId0", "d"."Id", "a"."Id", "e"."Id"
